.. _group___sys_graphic_itf:

=============
SysGraphicItf
=============

.. contents::
    :local:
    :depth: 1

Interface of SysGraphic.

Detailed Description
--------------------

The SysGraphic interface is projected to get access to the graphic library routines of a system. This is the system interface typically for the CODESYS target visualization.

**Copyright:**

Copyright (c) 2017-2020 CODESYS Development GmbH, Copyright (c) 1994-2016 3S-Smart Software Solutions GmbH. All rights reserved.

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga4a064b7c502a1f03e3c943a0e3973eb5:

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicGetDeviceContextForWindowDeviceContext (RTS_HANDLE hWindow, RTS_HANDLE hDCWindow, RTS_HANDLE *phDC)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Get a device context for an existing device context object belonging to a window. Remember to release such a device context using SysGraphicReleaseDeviceContextForWindowDeviceContext and not with SysGraphicDeleteDeviceContext or SysGraphicReleaseDeviceContext!

This method should be used when the SysWindow component wants to use SysGraphic methods directly. The intent of this method is to allow the SysWindow component to convert a system specific device context to a device context that the SysGraphic component can work with.

This can be necessary in the following situation:

  - SysWindow uses a system specific device context it received from the operating system

  - SysWindow wants to call methods from SysGraphic on this device context

  - The actual type SysGraphic uses for a device context is different than the operating system's type

The previous situation will work correctly only when both SysGraphic and SysWindow use the same data type for device contexts.

**Parameters**

+---------+-----------+---------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hWindow   | Handle to the actual window                       |
+---------+-----------+---------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hDCWindow | Handle to the device context of the actual window |
+---------+-----------+---------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | phDC      | Pointer to handle to get the device context       |
+---------+-----------+---------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga40fac78f1b984a54cd6ef762ea1bbe77:

^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Copies a bitmap from a source rectangle into a destination rectangle, stretching or compressing the bitmap to fit the dimensions of the destination rectangle, if necessary. | [in]    | rectSource      | Source rectangle                     |

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga9853f1793ae85562cf8d80846231ae95:

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicGetTextExtent (RTS_HANDLE hDC, void *pszText, RTS_UI32 ulDrawFlags, RTS_Size *pSize)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Function to calculate the size of a given text with the currently selected font. Use case (1): The function will treat the string as a single line string, i.e. it will cut the string after a possible linefeed and calculate the size of the first line only! Use case (2): The string will be formated and measured as defined by it's ulDrawFlags. Here, also text with flag TF_LINEBREAK will be measured, as it will be drawn. For using this case, the flag TF_MEASURE_ALL has to be used additional. And the paint rectangle size has to be forwarded by using pSize.

**Parameters**

+---------+-------------+---------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hDC         | Handle to device context                          |
+---------+-------------+---------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pszText     | Will be either:                                   |
|         |             |                                                   |
|         |             |   - charif TF_WSTRING is not set in ulDrawFlags   |
|         |             |                                                   |
|         |             |   - shortif (TF_WSTRING is set in ulDrawFlags)    |
+---------+-------------+---------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | ulDrawFlags | Draw flags. Defined in IEC-Code for Visualization |
+---------+-------------+---------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

error code

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicCreateBitmap (RTS_HANDLE hDC, const char *pszBmpPath, RTS_UI32 ulTransparentColor, RTS_UI32 ulFlags, RTS_HANDLE *phBitmap)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Function to create a Bitmap object(i.e. the HBITMAP in Win32)

**Parameters**

+---------+--------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hDC                | Handle to device context                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
+---------+--------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pszBmpPath         | The path of the bitmap to load. Please remark that no mapping of this path is done before this method is called! That means that it is up to the system specific implementation to respect possible mappings of paths that might be configured by the SysFile component. This mapping can be done by either using SysFileOpen for accessing files or by calling SysFileGetFullPath before passing the path to an operating system file implementation (like fopen or classes loading images directly like QImage from Qt or Bitmap from GDI+). |
+---------+--------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | ulTransparentColor | Contains the color that should be used as the transparent color. Will only be evaluated when the according flag is set. This color value can be used during loading an image when it is possible to do an optimization for painting transparent images like setting this color to transparent directly after loading or so. If such an optimization is not possible or not relevant, then the previous implementation by evaluating it within SysGraphicDrawBitmap can be used.                                                                |
+---------+--------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | ulFlags            | Flags. Defined in IEC-Code for Visualization. At the moment only the flag for transparency is relevant when loading an image!                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
+---------+--------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | phBitmap           | Pointer to get the bitmap handle                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
+---------+--------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

error code
**Note:**

Due to optimization reasons, the signature of this function was changed for the version 3.4.4. The transparency information is passed to this function too, to allow caching of transparency information. If you do not need to implement such a caching algorithm, then you can simply ignore the two parameters "ulFlags" and "ulTransparentColor".

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga93fc9d9c7aa0c8852a345d2e23b1b181:

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicBeginPaint (RTS_HANDLE hDC, RTS_HANDLE *phPaintContext)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

This function and SysGraphicEndPaint are used to encapsulate some paint calls together. An implementing platform could use this encapsulation for some optimizations. For every call to SysGraphicBeginPaint there will be an according call to SysGraphicEndPaint.

**Parameters**

+---------+----------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hDC            | The device context that will be drawn onto until the next call to SysGraphicEndPaint                                                                                  |
+---------+----------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | phPaintContext | An implementation could allocate some data and return it using this parameter. It will be given in the according call to SysGraphicEndPaint and can be deleted there. |
+---------+----------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1gaf302e17b875f61d1ae3baac9831a15e4:

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicEndPaint (RTS_HANDLE hDC, RTS_HANDLE hPaintContext)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

This function and SysGraphicBeginPaint are used to encapsulate some paint calls together. An implementing platform could use this encapsulation for some optimizations. For every call to SysGraphicBeginPaint there will be an according call to SysGraphicEndPaint.

| [in]    | hDC           | The device context that has been drawn onto until this call                        |
+---------+---------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga4c0d51f7be70c79f53a17d48c146b53c:

RTS_UI32 SysGraphicGetFeatureFlags (void)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

This function allows the SysGraphic implementation to give a hint to the kernel part of the target-visualization about some more or less optional feature that can be supported by an implementation. As this function was introduced later on, it should be included as an optional import to prevent inconsistencies. Additionally, calling code should assume a result of SYSGRAPHIC_FEATURES_ALL in case this function is not implemented for compatibility reasons.
**Returns:**

The optional features that are implemented by the current SysGraphic implementation as a combination of the flag values SYSGRAPHIC_FEATURES_...

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga5e5817bd44aebc91394f1c74ab68a3c7:

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicPreparePrinting (RTS_HANDLE hDC, RTS_HANDLE *phOptionalResultData, RTS_Rectangle *prWindow, RTS_Rectangle *prPrintOutput)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

This function can be used to prepare a device context for printing. Normally, this preparation is done by the assignment of a transformation so that the screen output is scaled correctly to a printer device context. This is perhaps necessary when the extent and/or the resolution of a printer device context is different than these properties of the screen device context.

**Parameters**

+---------+----------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hDC                  | The device context of the printer that has to be prepared by this call.                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
+---------+----------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | phOptionalResultData | An optional pointer to a handle that allows this method to allocate data that can be released later on in the call to SysGraphicFinishPrinting. If such data is not necessary on a specific platform implementation, this pointer can be NULL so that nothing can be returned here. |
+---------+----------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | prWindow             | A pointer to a rectangle that describes the extent of the target-visualization window on the screen.                                                                                                                                                                                |
+---------+----------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | prPrintOutput        | A pointer to a rectangle that describes the extent of the destination on the printer.                                                                                                                                                                                               |
+---------+----------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

An error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1gaaecddbc61733e95b7b10e70ce7aecef2:

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicFinishPrinting (RTS_HANDLE hDC, RTS_HANDLE hOptionalResultData)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

This function reverts the adaptations done by SysGraphicPreparePrinting

**Parameters**

+---------+---------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hDC                 | The device context of the printer that has to be reverted by this call.                                                                                     |
+---------+---------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hOptionalResultData | When SysGraphicPreparePrinting allocated and returned some additional data, this handle will be passed here again to be able to release the data correctly. |
+---------+---------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

An error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga782820e35db3bcf8c9da6a5ed21e1c0e:

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicSetAntiAliasingMode (RTS_HANDLE hDC, RTS_UI32 uiAntiAliasingSettings)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

This function assigns the anti-aliasing mode to a device context. By default, a device context should be in mode SYSGRAPHIC_ANTIALIASING_NONE. If a device does not support anti-aliased drawing, it should return ERR_NOT_SUPPORTED. To tell the programming system, whether the anti-aliasing feature is supported, the target-setting "visualization\targetsupport\targetvisualization_antialiasing" can be used.

**Parameters**

+---------+------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hDC                    | The device context to assign the anti-aliasing mode to.    |
+---------+------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | uiAntiAliasingSettings | The anti-aliasing mode (SYSGRAPHIC_ANTIALIASING_NONE,...). |
+---------+------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

An error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1gaaf724496eec95a23e49d9cb4b140c51a:

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicGetSysWindowFont (RTS_HANDLE hDC, RTS_HANDLE hSysGraphicFont, RTS_HANDLE *phSysWindowFont)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

This function is able to return the probably underlying font type as it is known by the SysWindow component from a font object that was allocated by the SysGraphic-Component.

**Parameters**

+---------+-----------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hDC             | The device context that should be used for the conversion of the font type.                                                                           |
+---------+-----------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hSysGraphicFont | The font that was allocated by the SysGraphic-Component and that should be converted to a font object that can be handled by the SysWindow-Component. |
+---------+-----------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | phSysWindowFont | A pointer that will receive the resulting (SysWindow) font.                                                                                           |
+---------+-----------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

An error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga2277a14c1ee963c5306c2c881a095c51:

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicInvalidateRectangle (RTS_HANDLE hDC, RTS_Rectangle rect)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

This function is optional and can be implemented by systems that need a valid back-buffer for painting to the foreground. This fact probably depends on the underlying graphics system (for Windows or native systems, this is probably not necessary, for QT based systems, an implementation might be necessary. The resulting list of invalidated rectangles should be reset in an implementation of SysGraphicResetInvalidation

**Parameters**

+---------+------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hDC  | The device context to invalidate in.                                                                                                                                                         |
+---------+------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | rect | The rectangle that is invalidated by the visualization. An implementation can use this call for example to fill a clip region so that only valid content will be drawn into the back-buffer. |
+---------+------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

An error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga209b5e9be7a1508a627cd4c65855f26a:

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicResetInvalidation (RTS_HANDLE hDC)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

This function is optional in the same way than SysGraphicInvalidateRectangle. Nevertheless, if SysGraphicInvalidateRectangle is implemented, then this function should be implemented too. It will be called to reset the list of passed invalidation rectangles. This fact probably depends on the underlying graphics system (for Windows or native systems, this is probably not necessary, for QT based systems, an implementation might be necessary.

**Parameters**

+---------+-----+--------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hDC | The device context to invalidate in. |
+---------+-----+--------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

An error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1gab4e06f08874da823a924b13228391f03:

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicInvalidateClientArea (RTS_HANDLE hDC)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

This function is optional, just as SysGraphicInvalidateRectangle, but should be implemented, if SysGraphicInvalidateRectangle is implemented. It will be called when the whole client area should be invalidated.

**Parameters**

+---------+-----+---------------------------------+
| [in]    | hDC | A handle to the device context. |
+---------+-----+---------------------------------+

**Returns:**

An error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga8a9e4f1d861e20593927748577f251a7:

RTS_HANDLE SysGraphicCreateTransformation (RTS_RESULT *pResult)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Creates an affine transformation object. Such transformations can be used for client local animations (e.g. when displaying the preview of multi-touch gestures) or for drawing transformed elements (e.g. rotated images or text). Usually such transformations are represented by transformation matrices. If affine transformations are not supported by the implementing platform,pResult should be set to ERR_NOTIMPLEMENTED. In such a situation, some features might not work correctly.

**Parameters**

+---------+---------+--------------------------------+
| [out]   | pResult | Optional pointer to error code |
+---------+---------+--------------------------------+

**Returns:**

A handle to the created transformation object

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga5b9675a578e8be1d9e64c11ca36eb073:

RTS_HANDLE SysGraphicCreateTransformationByValues (RTS_REAL32 m11, RTS_REAL32 m12, RTS_REAL32 m21, RTS_REAL32 m22, RTS_REAL32 dx, RTS_REAL32 dy, RTS_RESULT *pResult)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Creates an affine transformation object using the given matrix members. Such transformations can be used for client local animations (e.g. when displaying the preview of multi-touch gestures) or for drawing transformed elements (e.g. rotated images or text). Usually such transformations are represented by transformation matrices. If affine transformations are not supported by the implementing platform,pResult should be set to ERR_NOTIMPLEMENTED. In such a situation, some features might not work correctly.

**Parameters**

+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | m11     | The transformation matrix value in the first row, first column   |
+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | m12     | The transformation matrix value in the first row, second column  |
+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | m21     | The transformation matrix value in the second row, first column  |
+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | m22     | The transformation matrix value in the second row, second column |
+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | dx      | The transformation matrix value in the third row, first column   |
+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | dy      | The transformation matrix value in the third row, second column  |
+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | pResult | Optional pointer to error code                                   |
+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

A handle to the created transformation object

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga08a9f7b4037486e372a8954e7151dc9e:

+---------+------------+-------------------------------+

**Returns:**

An error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1gabfaaf78e208bd246010f49ede5b3c235:

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicTransformationScale (RTS_HANDLE hTransform, RTS_REAL32 x, RTS_REAL32 y)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Applies a scaling operation to the transformation object. The origin of the coordinate system (could have been moved by a previous call to SysGraphicTransformationTranslate will be used as the origin for the scaling operation.

**Parameters**

+---------+------------+----------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hTransform | The transformation to scale.                 |
+---------+------------+----------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | x          | The factor to scale in horizontal direction. |
+---------+------------+----------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | y          | The factor to scale in vertical direction.   |
+---------+------------+----------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

An error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1gaaa21188545a72b597d396a0fe05a78f4:

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicTransformationRotate (RTS_HANDLE hTransform, RTS_REAL32 angle)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Applies a rotation operation to the transformation object. The origin of the coordinate system (could have been moved by a previous call to SysGraphicTransformationTranslate will be used as the center for the rotation operation.

**Parameters**

+---------+------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hTransform | The transformation to rotate.                                                     |
+---------+------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | angle      | The angle of the rotation in degrees. Positive values specify clockwise rotation. |
+---------+------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

An error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga82856e23fdd3c2de0b1c202b6d276a78:

**Parameters**

+---------+------------+----------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hTransform | The transformation to translate.             |
+---------+------------+----------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | x          | The offset to shift in horizontal direction. |
+---------+------------+----------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | y          | The offset to shift in vertical direction.   |
+---------+------------+----------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

An error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga7ddaf9233f7b58f511e59ddcf83ccbaf:

RTS_RESULT SysGraphicSetActiveTransformation (RTS_HANDLE hdc, RTS_HANDLE hTransform)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Activates an affine transformation object on the given device context. This transformation will be applied to modify all follow up drawing operations on this device context until a different (or no) transformation is set.

**Parameters**

+---------+------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hdc        | The device context to apply the transformation on.                                      |
+---------+------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hTransform | The transformation to apply. Pass RTS_INVALID_HANDLE to deactivate any transformations. |
+---------+------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

An error code

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga4330b069437a1f23f4871ce0d1e08b09:

RTS_HANDLE SysGraphicGetActiveTransformation (RTS_HANDLE hdc, RTS_RESULT *pResult)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Returns the currently active affine transformation object on the given device context.

**Parameters**

+---------+------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hdc        | The device context to retrieve the transformation from.                                 |
+---------+------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hTransform | The transformation to apply. Pass RTS_INVALID_HANDLE to deactivate any transformations. |
+---------+------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | pResult    | Optional pointer to error code                                                          |
+---------+------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

The handle or the active transformation or RTS_INVALID_HANDLE if there was no active one..

.. _group___sys_graphic_itf_1ga8d9cdfa3bc890e30429817b6bf3f6872:

| [out]   | pResult    | Optional pointer to error code.  |

**Returns:**
